<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vrintlec</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vriendelijc</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*friuntlik</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*friuntlik</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*frijōndlīkaz</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:equivalent.html>equivalent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vriend.html>vriend</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-lijk</i>. ***vriendin.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vriendin.html>vriendin</a> (528)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vriendinne</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:equivalent.html>Equivalent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vriend.html>vriend</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-in</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vriendin.html>vriendin</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vriendinnen.html>vriendinnen</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vriendinnetje.html>vriendinnetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:masculine.html>masculine</a></i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vriend.html>vriend</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vriezen.html>vriezen</a> (13324)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vriesen</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*friesan</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*freusan</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*freusaną</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*prews-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb"><a href = vnd.unilang:verb.html>Verb</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:first.html>First</a> attested <a href = vnd.unilang:around.html>around</a> 1783. <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vrij.html>vrij</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:korps.html>korps</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:probably.html>probably</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> calque <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a>  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Freikorps</i>, attested <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:few.html>few</a> years earlier.
</p>

</p>

<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uw.html>uw</a> <b>Vrijcorps</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:steeds.html>steeds</a> blijv' <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> ſtand, / <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>Tot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nut.html>nut</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stad.html>Stad</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vaderland.html>Vaderland</a>.</dd></dl></li>

Wolff</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:vrijheid.html>Vrijheid</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:blijheid.html>blijheid</a>: Vaderlansch dichtstuk</i>, publ. <a href = vnd.unilang:by.html>by</a> Isaac <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Cleef, <a href = vnd.unilang:page.html>page</a> 19.
